# Patch Notes

## Summary
- Uniques: 16 added, 9 removed, 1254 modified
- Sets: 1 added, 0 removed, 37 modified
- Runewords: 0 added, 0 removed, 71 modified
- Base Items: 0 added, 0 removed, 36 modified
